date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

Based on:
<div class="references" markdown="1">
- https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
- https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html.
</div>

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="455" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="459" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="467" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="483" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="488" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="495" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="510" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#518" class="Function">_</a> <a id="520" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="522" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="526" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="799" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#806" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="816" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="825" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="891" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="957" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<a id="1525" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="⊥"></a><a id="1530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1530" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1533" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1547" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1860" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1918" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1934" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1943" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1951" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1959" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1974" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1984" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1988" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2003" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2346" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2353" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
<a id="2360" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ"></a><a id="2367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2369" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2389" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2391" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2406" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2415" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2419" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2425" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="2433" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2451" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="Σ.fst"></a><a id="2461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a>

<a id="2485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="2492" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3099" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3117" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3407" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3430" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3441" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3455" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3455" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3464" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3468" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3486" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3608" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3625" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

### Identity Type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5029" class="Comment">-- Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle</a>

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6303" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6303" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6314" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6316" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6317" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6320" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6322" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6324" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6325" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6317" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6336" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6338" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6339" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6341" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6325" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6320" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6354" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6477" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6303" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6501" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7171" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7178" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7178" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7199" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7201" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7203" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7204" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7206" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7199" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7217" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7767" class="Comment">-- Equality.</a>

<a id="7781" class="Comment">-- Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this</a>
<a id="7849" class="Comment">-- is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this</a>
<a id="7917" class="Comment">-- is the symmetric property of equality.</a>
<a id="inv"></a><a id="7959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7959" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="7963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7965" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="7967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7967" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="7968" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7970" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7971" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7973" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7967" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="7981" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="7984" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7985" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7985" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="7987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7987" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="7989" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7971" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7992" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="7996" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7998" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7985" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8000" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8003" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7987" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8007" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7987" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8011" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7985" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7959" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5188" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8026" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8026" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8029" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8031" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5188" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8036" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8026" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="8039" class="Comment">-- Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions</a>
<a id="8107" class="Comment">-- preserve equalities.</a>
<a id="ap"></a><a id="8131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8131" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="8134" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8136" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8148" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8138" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="8157" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8159" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8160" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8160" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8162" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8164" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8169" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8141" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="8171" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8174"   <a id="8213" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8187" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8217" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8175" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8187" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8177" class="Bound">b</a>

<a id="9260" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9265" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8371" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

  <a id="14215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14095" class="Function">∘-lassoc</a> <a id="14224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14228" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14230" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5188" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="14237" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14240" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14242" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14246" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14247" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14250" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14228" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14252" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14240" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14253" class="Symbol">)))</a>

    <a id="14301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14302" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14306" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14281" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14308" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14283" class="Bound">D</a><a id="14311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14313" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14315" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14316" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14279" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14322" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14324" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14281" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14325" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14327" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14329" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14330" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14332" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14277" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14336" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14338" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14279" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14339" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14341" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="14347" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14302" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14353" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14316" class="Bound">g</a><a id="14354" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14330" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14359" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14361" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14302" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14369" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14316" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14330" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14375" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="14380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14260" class="Function">∘-rassoc</a> <a id="14389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14389" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14391" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14393" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14395" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7959" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="14401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14095" class="Function">∘-lassoc</a> <a id="14411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14389" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14391" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14415" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14393" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14416" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="14419" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14055" class="Module">Composition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14591" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14598" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14607" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14608" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14608" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14611" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14613" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14615" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14616" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14618" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14620" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14608" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14627" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14629" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14630" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14632" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14634" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14616" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14636" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14638" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14643" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14611" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14645" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14647" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14655" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14733" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14773" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14785" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14785" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14787" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14787" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14789" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14791" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14793" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14793" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14797" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14616" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14798" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14800" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14802" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14630" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14804" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14793" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14805" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14808" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14608" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14819" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14821" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14611" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14823" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14827" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14773" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14836" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14836" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14838" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14838" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14840" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14842" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14843" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14845" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14847" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14616" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14848" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14850" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14836" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14854" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14843" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14856" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14859" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14838" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14861" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14843" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="14915" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14915" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14866" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="14919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14919" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14921" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14773" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14915" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14919" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="14939" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

  <a id="17129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7537" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Fibers

Contractible types with a center of contraction.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17217" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Fibers"></a><a id="17224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17224" class="Module">Fibers</a> <a id="17231" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17232" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="17235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17235" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="17237" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17240" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="17242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="17249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17232" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="17251" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17253" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17254" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17254" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="17256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17258" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="17263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17235" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="17265" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="17268" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Contractible types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17746" class="Comment">-- Contractible.  Contractible types with a center of contraction.</a>
<a id="17813" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Contractible"></a><a id="17820" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17820" class="Module">Contractible</a> <a id="17833" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="17842" class="Comment">-- Contractible types. A contractible type is a type such that every</a>
  <a id="17913" class="Comment">-- element is equal to a center of contraction.</a>

## Equivalence in HoTT

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18123" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Equivalence"></a><a id="18130" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18130" class="Module">Equivalence</a> <a id="18142" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="18151" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="18158" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18158" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="18182" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18183" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18183" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18188" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18190" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18191" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18193" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18195" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18183" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="18202" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18204" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18205" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18216" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18218" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="18228" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18296" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18361" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18378" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18389" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18391" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18392" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18394" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18191" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18398" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18400" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18205" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18401" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18403" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18410" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18183" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18414" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18418" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="18424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18378" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18435" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18437" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18440" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18440" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="18442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18205" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18445" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18447" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18449" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17963" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="18457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17326" class="Function">fib</a> <a id="18462" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18435" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18464" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18440" class="Bound">b</a><a id="18465" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18472" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18543" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isEquiv"></a><a id="18586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18586" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="18594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18597" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18597" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18601" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18191" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18603" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18205" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18606" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18608" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18610" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18615" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18183" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18619" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18623" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="18629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18586" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="18637" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18639" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18378" class="Function">isContrMap</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21895" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="21902" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21902" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="21919" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21920" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="21923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21923" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="21925" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21927" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21928" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="21937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21920" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="21939" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21941" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21942" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21942" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="21944" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21946" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="21951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21923" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="21953" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21955" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="21964" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22031" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22077" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22077" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22095" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22097" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22098" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22098" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22100" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="22102" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21928" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="22108" href="{% endraw %}{% link ## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23080" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23087" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23105" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23106" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23107" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23109" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23118" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23189" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23227" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23227" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23233" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23235" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23236" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23238" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23106" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23246" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23248" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23250" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23106" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

<a id="23792" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23797" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23087" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24027" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24034" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24047" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24056" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24125" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24147" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24149" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24151" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24151" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24152" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24156" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24156" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24158" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24160" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24165" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24151" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24166" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24168" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24170" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24175" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24151" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24179" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24186" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24188" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24190" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24192" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24194" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24194" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24196" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24198" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24186" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24199" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24201" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24203" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24192" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24194" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24209" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24214" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24249" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24255" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24257" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24259" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24259" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24260" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24269" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24270" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24275" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24259" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24276" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24249" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24287" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24288" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24290" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24292" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24295" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24300" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24287" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24301" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24303" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24314" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24380" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24398" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24405" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24407" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24409" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24409" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24412" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24414" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24416" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24418" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24419" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24421" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24428" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24409" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24430" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24432" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24435" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24419" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24443" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24412" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24450" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24463" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24465" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24465" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24419" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24470" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24472" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24482" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24435" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24465" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24485" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24497" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24499" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24499" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24501" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24503" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24419" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24504" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24506" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24508" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24435" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24499" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24511" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24515" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24398" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24522" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24522" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24530" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24532" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20225" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24541" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24543" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24545" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24547" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24522" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24553" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24559" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24561" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24530" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24565" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24570" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24628" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24640" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24642" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24644" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24647" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24647" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24649" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24651" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24654" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24654" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24663" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24644" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24665" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24667" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24669" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24647" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24681" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24697" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24699" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24654" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24708" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24710" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24717" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24719" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24140" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24729" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24654" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24733" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24734" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24798" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24803" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24034" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25011" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25018" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25023" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25032" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25103" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

<a id="25718" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25018" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="27986" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="27991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27204" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28235" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28242" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28242" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28255" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28256" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28259" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28259" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28261" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28264" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28266" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28268" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28273" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28256" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28275" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28277" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28278" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28282" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28259" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28291" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28300" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28331" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28338" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28338" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28344" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28345" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28345" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28347" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28264" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28353" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28278" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28354" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28356" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28363" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28256" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28367" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28259" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28373" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31092" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31099" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31099" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31113" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31114" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31117" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31119" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31121" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31122" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31124" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31114" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31133" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31135" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31136" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31138" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31145" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31117" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31147" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31149" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33845" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

   <a id="35253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7592" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
     <a id="35264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35269" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34710" class="Function">compEqv</a> <a id="35277" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35236" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="35279" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34922" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35236" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35288" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="35291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7438" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35295" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5188" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="35300" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="35302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7438" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35309" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34922" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35236" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35322" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35324" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35236" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35336" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7438" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35340" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20225" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19494" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35236" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35365" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7438" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7537" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35381" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35384" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34130" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35588" class="Comment">-- module Univalence where</a>
<a id="35615" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="35618" class="Comment">--   -- Voevodsky&#39;s Univalence Axiom.</a>
<a id="35656" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceAxiom {ℓ} {A B : Type ℓ} where</a>
<a id="35709" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv : A == B → A ≃ B</a>
<a id="35741" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv p = qinv-≃</a>
<a id="35767" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) p)</a>
<a id="35800" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) (inv p) , (transport-inv-l p , transport-inv-r p))</a>
<a id="35881" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="35884" class="Comment">--     -- The Univalence axiom induces an equivalence between equalities</a>
<a id="35957" class="Comment">--     -- and equivalences.</a>
<a id="35985" class="Comment">--     postulate axiomUnivalence : isEquiv idtoeqv</a>
<a id="36036" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence : (A == B) ≃ (A ≃ B)</a>
<a id="36078" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence = idtoeqv , axiomUnivalence</a>
<a id="36127" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36130" class="Comment">--     -- Introduction rule for equalities.</a>
<a id="36174" class="Comment">--     ua : A ≃ B → A == B</a>
<a id="36201" class="Comment">--     ua = remap eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36233" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36236" class="Comment">--     -- Computation rules</a>
<a id="36264" class="Comment">--     ua-β : (eqv : A ≃ B) → idtoeqv (ua eqv) == eqv</a>
<a id="36318" class="Comment">--     ua-β eqv = lrmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36364" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36367" class="Comment">--     ua-η : (p : A == B) → ua (idtoeqv p) == p</a>
<a id="36416" class="Comment">--     ua-η p = rlmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36460" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceAxiom public</a>
<a id="36493" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36496" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36499" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36538" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36599" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36648" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36667" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36682" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36747" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36800" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36818" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36829" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36832" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="36904" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="36929" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37025" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37046" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37061" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37168" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37273" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37352" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37428" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37511" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37534" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37545" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37560" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37646" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37675" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37694" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37782" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37892" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37980" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38023" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38039" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38042" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38076" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38156" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38176" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38191" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38261" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38326" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38375" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38393" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="38404" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38407" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="38482" class="Comment">--     ua-inv α =</a>
<a id="38500" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38515" class="Comment">--         ua (invEqv α)                       ==⟨ ap (_· ua (invEqv α)) (inv (·-linv (ua α))) ⟩</a>
<a id="38612" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · ua α · ua (invEqv α)   ==⟨ ·-assoc (inv (ua α)) _ _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38690" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · (ua α · ua (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap (inv (ua α) ·_) (ua-inv-r α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38775" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · refl _                 ==⟨ inv (·-runit (inv ((ua α)))) ⟩</a>
<a id="38857" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="38879" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="38890" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceLemmas public</a>
<a id="38924" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38927" class="Comment">-- open Univalence</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
